***wal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a> (6453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vallum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vallus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stake, <a href = vnd.unilang:palisade.html>palisade</a>, point</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wall</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wallen.html>wallen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>walletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>coast, shore (side of <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> near to the water)</li>
<li>earthen levee as protection against flooding</li>
<li>wall around city as military defense</li>
<li>periorbital dark circle</li>
<li>eye circle; <a href = vnd.unilang:bags.html>bags</a></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">levee</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dijk.html>dijk</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">defensive wall</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omwalling.html>omwalling</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stadsmuur.html>stadsmuur</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">eye <a href = vnd.unilang:bags.html>bags</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">oogwal</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwalaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">whale</i>. Possibly to avoid confusion with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wall; shore</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the derived compound word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:walvis.html>walvis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale; <a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a>. whale-fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> gained currency <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Similar clarifying compounds can be found elsewhere in Dutch: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraanvogel.html>kraanvogel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crane; <a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a>. crane-bird</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muildier.html>muildier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mule; <a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a>. mule-animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oeros.html>oeros</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">auroch; auroch-ox</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rendier.html>rendier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rein; <a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a>. rein-animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tortelduif.html>tortelduif</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turtle (bird); <a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a>. turtle <a href = vnd.unilang:dove.html>dove</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:windhond.html>windhond</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">greyhound; <a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a>. wind-dog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wallen.html>wallen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>walletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***waldo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:waldo.html>waldo</a> (19277)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the Robert A. Heinlein story <i><a href = vnd.unilang:waldo.html>Waldo</a></i>, published in <i>Astounding</i> in 1940, derived from the name of the eponymous protagonist, <a href = vnd.unilang:waldo.html>Waldo</a> F. Jones, who invented remote <a href = vnd.unilang:manipulators.html>manipulators</a> to overcome his own <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/myasthenia_gravis" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:myasthenia gravis">myasthenia gravis</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:waldo.html>waldo</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">waldos</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">waldoes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A remote manipulation system in which a slave device mimics the motions of a master device manipulated directly by the operator.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1940</b>,  Robert A. Heinlein,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:waldo.html>Waldo</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:waldo.html>Waldo</a> flexed and extended his <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a> gently; the two <a href = vnd.unilang:pairs.html>pairs</a> of <b>waldoes</b> in the screen followed in exact, simultaneous parallelism.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Remote_manipulator" class="extiw" title="w:Remote manipulator">Remote <a href = vnd.unilang:manipulator.html>manipulator</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Remote_manipulator" class="extiw" title="w:Remote manipulator">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:walgden.html>walgden</a> (86234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:walgen.html>walgen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*walgon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*walgōną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">used with <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to abhor, to hate
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:walg.html>walg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> I <b>abhor</b> you.</dd></dl></li></ol>

***walkie-talkie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:walkie-talkie.html>walkie-talkie</a> (20904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">walking</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">talking</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:walkie-talkie.html>walkie-talkie</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:walkie-talkies.html>walkie-talkies</a></b>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Portable_radio_SCR536.png/150px-Portable_radio_SCR536.png" decoding="async" width="150" height="242" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Portable_radio_SCR536.png/225px-Portable_radio_SCR536.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Portable_radio_SCR536.png/300px-Portable_radio_SCR536.png 2x" data-file-width="432" data-file-height="696" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:walkie-talkie.html>walkie-talkie</a></div></div></div>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:portable.html>portable</a>, bi-directional radio transceiver, usually as a pair.
<ul><li>2009, L. K. Bandyopadhyay, ‎S. K. Chaulya, ‎P. K. Mishra, <i>Wireless Communication in Underground Mines: RFID-based Sensor Networking</i>, Springer, →ISBN
<dl><dd>A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:walkie-talkie.html>walkie-talkie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a handheld, <a href = vnd.unilang:portable.html>portable</a>, two-way radio transceiver. It includes a half-duplex channel (only one radio transmits at a time, though any number can listen) and a push-to-talk switch that <a href = vnd.unilang:starts.html>starts</a> transmission.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A walk and talk.
<ul><li>1947, Nero Wolfe, <i>Too Many Women: A Nero Wolfe Novel</i>:
<dl><dd>It could be that her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:walkie-talkie.html>walkie-talkie</a></b> with Naylor <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> concerned a private matter not connected with what <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> about to happen to him, ...</dd></dl></li>
<li>1993, B. Kaye Olson, <i>Energy <a href = vnd.unilang:secrets.html>Secrets</a> for Tired Mothers on the Run</i>, Health Communications, →ISBN, page 153:
<dl><dd>Go on a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:walkie-talkie.html>walkie-talkie</a></b>. Everyone goes on a 15-minute brisk walk and talks about their day.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***walrus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:walrus.html>walrus</a> (22958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The origin of this word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not wholly certain, with several <a href = vnd.unilang:theories.html>theories</a> proposed. Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hvalros</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">valross</i>, from an inversion of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hrosshvalr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse-whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale; large sea-animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ros.html>ros</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> word may, however, <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> a folk-etymological modification of Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">rossmal</i>, related to Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rusta-</i>, from the <a href = vnd.unilang:rust.html>rust</a> colour of the animal.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Preference for borrowing the inverted form could have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> due to the influence of the already existing Dutch compound <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:walvis.html>walvis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale-fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:walrus.html>walrus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:walrussen.html>walrussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:walrus.html>walrusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:walrus.html>walrus</a></span>, any member of the family Odobenidae of which <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Odobenus_rosmarus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Odobenus rosmarus"><i>Odobenus rosmarus</i></a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the sole extant member</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:walrus.html>walrus</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:zoogdieren.html>zoogdieren</a>)</span> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Odobenus_rosmarus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Odobenus rosmarus"><span style="color:green;"><i>Odobenus rosmarus</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" />, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> vinpotig <a href = vnd.unilang:zoogdier.html>zoogdier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sterke.html>sterke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beneden.html>beneden</a> gerichte <a href = vnd.unilang:hoektanden.html>hoektanden</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:walrus.html>walrus</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> lievelingsdier.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Afgeleide_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:afgeleide.html>Afgeleide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>

***walvis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:walvis.html>walvis</a> (5878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">walvisch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">walvisk</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, presumably to clarify the meaning. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vis.html>vis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Old Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>wal</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwalaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)kʷálos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sheatfish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">waldier</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:walrus.html>walrus</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">grindewal</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">walfisk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Walfisch</i>. The simple form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> cognate with German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wal.html>Wal</a></i>, English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">whale</i>, Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hval</i>, Swedish <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>val</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:walvis.html>walvis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:walvissen.html>walvissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:walvis.html>walvisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>whale, mammal of the order Cetacea</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wam.html>wam</a> (78198)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wamme</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wam.html>wam</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly; stomach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wamba</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly; body</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wambō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly, stomach, abdomen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wamp-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">membrane (of bowels), intestines, womb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wambuis.html>wambuis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gambeson</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wamb</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buis.html>buis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jacket, cover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">womb</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:wam.html>wam</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">wame</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">womb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wamme</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wampe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">paunch, belly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">vom</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly, paunch, rumen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">våmb</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly, stomach, rumen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">vomb</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">vömb</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly, abdomen, stomach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wam.html>wam</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wam.html>wammen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wam.html>wammetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a belly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a stomach</li>
<li>a beef dewlap</li>
<li>a fish belly cut open</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">wambais</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">wambeis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">doublet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">wamba</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stomach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wam.html>wam</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">belly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***wand.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wand.html>wand</a> (10587)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">want</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wanduz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wickerwork; barrier, fence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wand.html>Wand</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wandelen.html>wandelen</a> (2253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wandelen.html>wandelen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wandalon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wandlōną</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wandelen.html>wandelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to stroll, be on a walk (‘to go for a walk’ = ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wandelen.html>wandelen</a>’)</li>
<li>to walk</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wanneer.html>wanneer</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wan <a href = vnd.unilang:eer.html>eer</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wan ēr</i>. The former part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> found as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwan</i>. The latter part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> identical with modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eer.html>eer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">before</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">wannehr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">wéini</i>, obsolete <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wannehe</i>.

<p>Unknown. The only cognate found <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">waarje</i>.

***warenhuis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:warenhuis.html>warenhuis</a> (10295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">goods</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Warenhaus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:warenhuis.html>warenhuis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:warenhuizen.html>warenhuizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:warenhuis.html>warenhuisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A department store.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">warenmagazijn</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A warehouse.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pakhuis.html>pakhuis</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A greenhouse in which crop rotation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> practised.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***warlock.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:warlock.html>warlock</a> (50298)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">warloghe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">warlowe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">warloȝe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wǣrloga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">traitor, deceiver</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">truce-breaker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wǣr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:convenant.html>covenant</a>, truce, pact, promise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">true</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vērus</i>) + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">loga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">liar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lugô</i>, related to Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">lēogan</i> (whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lie</i>). The hard <i>-ck</i> ending originated in Scottish and Northern English, like the sense "male magic-user" (from the notion that such <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> in league with the Devil). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">wārlogo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">truce-breaker, traitor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>A few writers alternatively propose derivation from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">varðlokkur</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">caller of <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>spirits</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> but as the <i>OED</i> notes, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> implausible due to the extreme rarity of the <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> word and because forms without hard <i>-k</i>, which are consistent with the Old English etymology (“traitor”), are attested earlier than forms with <i>-k</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> and forms with <i>-ð-</i> are not attested.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:warlock.html>warlock</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">warlocks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A male magic-user; a male witch.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Because of its etymology, the term <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not used by some male witches, who prefer other <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> like <i>witch</i> instead.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-5"> | 5 | </a></sup></li></ul>
</body>
